A person can understand himself and what he is simply by understanding the first lessons of the Bhagavad-gÄ«tÄ (2.13):

â€œAs the embodied soul continuously passes, in this body, from boyhood to youth to old age, the soul similarly passes into another body at death. A sober person is not bewildered by such a change.â€

(32) One should not fight or quarrel before the Deity.
